<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to Run</h2><a id="user-content-how-to-run" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to Run" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#how-to-run"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1 — Create a New Kaggle Notebook</h3><a id="user-content-step-1--create-a-new-kaggle-notebook" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1 — Create a New Kaggle Notebook" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#step-1--create-a-new-kaggle-notebook"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Go to <a href="https://www.kaggle.com/" rel="nofollow">kaggle.com</a>, click <strong>Create → New Notebook</strong>, and upload <code>GNN_Final_Code.ipynb</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2 — Add the Dataset</h3><a id="user-content-step-2--add-the-dataset" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2 — Add the Dataset" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#step-2--add-the-dataset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In the notebook, click the <strong>+ Add Data</strong> icon in the right panel → search for <strong>"Elliptic Bitcoin Dataset"</strong> → add it. This makes the three CSV files available at:</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3 — Set the Accelerator to T4 x2 GPU</h3><a id="user-content-step-3--set-the-accelerator-to-t4-x2-gpu" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3 — Set the Accelerator to T4 x2 GPU" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#step-3--set-the-accelerator-to-t4-x2-gpu"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Go to <strong>Settings (right panel) → Accelerator → GPU T4 x2</strong>. This is required — training will be extremely slow without it.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 4 — Run All Cells</h3><a id="user-content-step-4--run-all-cells" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 4 — Run All Cells" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#step-4--run-all-cells"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Click <strong>Run All</strong> (or go to <strong>Run → Run All</strong>). All dependencies (PyTorch Geometric etc.) are installed inside the notebook itself, so no manual installs are needed.</p>
<p dir="auto">That's it. Total runtime is approximately <strong>45 mins</strong> on T4 x2.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Models Trained &amp; Results</h2><a id="user-content-models-trained--results" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Models Trained &amp; Results" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#models-trained--results"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Four models are benchmarked on the Elliptic Bitcoin Dataset (Bitcoin transaction fraud detection):</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table data-catalyst=""><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Model</th>
<th>Macro F1</th>
<th>PR-AUC</th>
<th>Illicit Recall</th>
<th>FPR</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ResGCN</td>
<td>0.7200</td>
<td>0.3681</td>
<td>0.5202</td>
<td>0.0411</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ImprovedGAT</td>
<td>0.7112</td>
<td>0.4306</td>
<td>0.4338</td>
<td>0.0293</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>GraphSAGE Ensemble</td>
<td>0.7607</td>
<td>0.4239</td>
<td>0.5119</td>
<td>0.0221</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>XGBoost (baseline)</td>
<td>0.8699</td>
<td>0.7073</td>
<td>0.6206</td>
<td>0.0018</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">XGBoost achieves the highest overall scores because the dataset includes 72 pre-engineered structural features that already encode graph neighbourhood statistics — giving tree-based models an inherent advantage on this specific benchmark. Despite receiving only 94 of 166 features, GNNs learn comparable structural patterns purely through message passing and achieve higher illicit recall sensitivity in some configurations.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Method</h2><a id="user-content-method" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Method" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#method"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Bitcoin transactions are modelled as a directed graph where each node is a transaction and each edge is a fund flow. Three GNN architectures are trained alongside an XGBoost baseline:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>ResGCN</strong> — standard graph convolution with residual skip connections to prevent vanishing gradients</li>
<li><strong>ImprovedGAT</strong> — attention-based aggregation that learns which neighbouring transactions are most suspicious</li>
<li><strong>GraphSAGE Ensemble</strong> — three models trained with different random seeds, probabilities averaged for stability</li>
<li><strong>XGBoost</strong> — tabular baseline with no graph awareness, trained on all 166 features</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Key implementation choices:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>GNNs receive only 94 local features; graph structure is learned via message passing (the 72 pre-engineered structural features are withheld to test whether GNNs can learn them automatically)</li>
<li>Strict time-based train/val/test split (timesteps 1–34 / 35–38 / 39–49) to simulate real-world deployment on future transactions</li>
<li>Focal Loss + inverse-frequency class weights to handle the severe 10:1 licit-to-illicit imbalance</li>
<li>Decision threshold tuned on the validation set instead of using a fixed 0.5 cutoff</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Interpreting the Results</h2><a id="user-content-interpreting-the-results" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Interpreting the Results" href="https://github.com/MandalRounak/Winter-projects-25-26/blob/main/GNN%20Learning%20Path%20%26%20Fraud%20Detection%20System/End_term/GNN_group6_Rounak_240885/README_Group6.md#interpreting-the-results"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Standard accuracy is meaningless here — a model predicting "licit" for everything scores ~95% while catching zero fraud. Macro F1 and PR-AUC are the real metrics.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>XGBoost dominates</strong> on F1 and PR-AUC because it receives all 166 features including the pre-engineered structural ones, giving it relational information for free. Its FPR of 0.0018 means very few false alarms — it is highly precise.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>GNNs are more sensitive</strong> — GraphSAGE Ensemble catches 51% of illicit transactions vs XGBoost's 62%, but with only 94 features and no hand-crafted graph statistics. This demonstrates that message passing genuinely learns network structure rather than just memorising node features. GNNs also have a higher FPR, meaning more false alarms.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>The practical takeaway:</strong> XGBoost is better when minimising false alarms matters (reducing investigator workload). GNNs are better when missing an illicit transaction is the costlier mistake. In a real AML system, both would run together.</p>

</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>
